<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0 Transitional//EN"><html lang="en-US"><head><title>EdgarFiling</title><meta content="text/html; charset=windows-1252"><meta name="GENERATOR" content="MSHTML 8.00.7601.18094"></head><body bgcolor="#ffffff"><p style="text-align: right;"><strong>Exhibit 99</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>ADP Reports Second Quarter Fiscal 2017 Results</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><p><ul type="disc"><li>Revenues increased 6% to $3.0 billion for the quarter, 7% on a constant dollar basis<br></li><li>Diluted earnings per share from continuing operations increased 53% to $1.13; adjusted diluted earnings per share from continuing operations increased 20% to $0.87, 19% on a constant dollar basis</li><li>On November 28, 2016, ADP completed the sale of its Consumer Health Spending Account (&#8220;CHSA&#8221;) and Consolidated Omnibus Reconciliation Act (&#8220;COBRA&#8221;) businesses for a pre-tax gain of $205 million</li><li>ADP acquired 4.6 million shares of its stock for treasury at a cost of $422 million in the quarter</li></ul><p>ROSELAND, N.J., Feb.  01, 2017  (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- ADP&#174; (Nasdaq:ADP), a leading global provider of Human Capital Management (HCM) solutions, today announced its second quarter fiscal 2017 financial results, and provided an update to its fiscal 2017 outlook.&#160;</p><p><strong>Second Quarter Fiscal 2017 Consolidated Results</strong></p><p>Compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter, revenues grew 6% to $3.0 billion, 7% on a constant dollar basis.&#160; Net earnings from continuing operations grew 50% to $511 million, 49% on a constant dollar basis.&#160; Adjusted EBIT grew 17% to $593 million, 16% on a constant dollar basis.&#160; Adjusted EBIT margin increased about 180 basis points in the quarter to 19.8% driven by operational efficiencies and slower growth in our selling expenses.&#160; Diluted earnings per share from continuing operations increased to $1.13, representing growth of 53% on a reported and constant dollar basis.&#160; Adjusted diluted earnings per share from continuing operations increased 20% to $0.87, 19% on a constant dollar basis, and included a $0.01 tax benefit related to the adoption of new stock-based compensation accounting guidance.&#160;</p><p>Constant dollar, adjusted EBIT, adjusted EBIT margin and adjusted diluted earnings per share are non-GAAP financial measures.&#160; For ADP&#8217;s definition of adjusted EBIT, see the paragraph &#8220;Non-GAAP Financial Information&#8221; at the end of this release.&#160; Please refer to the accompanying financial tables for a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures to their comparable GAAP measures.</p><p>&#8220;Overall, I am pleased with ADP&#8217;s second quarter results which demonstrate the strength and stability of our business model. &#160;We believe the client experience is a key component of our success and that our investments and strategic initiatives are continuing to have a positive impact on our business performance,&#8221; said Carlos Rodriguez, president and chief executive officer, ADP.&#160;&#160;</p><p>&#8220;ADP&#8217;s results reflect solid performance despite pressure from new business bookings which declined 5% compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter,&#8221; said Jan Siegmund, chief financial officer, ADP.&#160;&#160;&#8220;This decline was driven by the continued difficult grow-over related to the tailwinds from our fiscal 2016 sales of additional modules related to the Affordable Care Act, and an elevated level of buyer uncertainty around the November U.S. elections. &#160;While below our expectations for the second quarter, we believe this new business bookings pressure will begin to subside as the year progresses.&#8221;</p><p><strong>Second Quarter Fiscal 2017 Segment Results</strong></p><p><u>Employer Services</u> &#8211; Employer Services offers a comprehensive range of HCM and human resources outsourcing solutions.</p><ul type="disc"><li>Employer Services revenues increased 4% on a reported and constant dollar basis when compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter.</li><li>The number of employees on ADP clients' payrolls in the United States increased 2.3% for the second quarter when measured on a same-store-sales basis for a subset of clients ranging from small to large businesses.</li><li>Employer Services client revenue retention was up 10 basis points compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter.</li><li>Employer Services segment margin increased approximately 150 basis points compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter.&#160; This increase was primarily driven by operational efficiencies and slower growth in our selling expenses.</li></ul><p><u>PEO Services</u> &#8211; PEO Services provides comprehensive employment administration outsourcing solutions through a co-employment relationship.</p><ul type="disc"><li>PEO Services revenues increased 12% compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter.</li><li>PEO Services segment margin increased approximately 120 basis points compared to last year&#8217;s second quarter, primarily driven by operational efficiencies and slower growth in our selling expenses.&#160;</li><li>Average worksite employees paid by PEO Services increased 12% for the quarter to approximately 452,000.</li></ul><p><u>Interest on Funds Held for Clients</u> &#8211; The safety, liquidity and diversification of ADP clients&#8217; funds are the foremost objectives of the company&#8217;s investment strategy.&#160; Client funds are invested in accordance with ADP&#8217;s prudent and conservative investment guidelines and the credit quality of the investment portfolio is predominantly AAA/AA.</p><ul type="disc"><li>For the second quarter, interest on funds held for clients increased 3% to $92 million from $89 million a year ago.</li><li>Average client funds balances increased 2% in the second quarter to $20.9 billion compared to $20.5 billion a year ago.&#160;</li><li>The average interest yield on client funds was 1.8% which was about flat compared to a year ago.</li></ul><p><strong>Notable Subsequent Events</strong></p><p>In January 2017, ADP acquired The Marcus Buckingham Company, Inc. for total cash consideration at closing of approximately $70 million, and contingent consideration of up to $35 million, which is payable over the next three years, subject to the achievement of specified financial metrics and/or other conditions.</p><p><strong>Fiscal 2017 Outlook</strong></p><p>Certain components of ADP&#8217;s fiscal 2017 outlook and related growth comparisons exclude the impact of the following items and are discussed on an adjusted basis where applicable.&#160; Please refer to the accompanying financial tables for a reconciliation of these adjusted amounts to their closest comparable GAAP measure.</p><ul type="disc"><li>Fiscal 2016 first quarter pre-tax gain on sale of the AdvancedMD business of $29 million</li><li>Fiscal 2016 second quarter pre-tax gain on sale of a building of $14 million</li><li>Fiscal 2016 fourth quarter pre-tax workforce optimization charge of $48 million</li><li>Fiscal 2017 pre-tax restructuring charges of approximately $90 million, $41 million of which occurred in the first half of the fiscal year, with the remaining $49 million expected to occur in the latter part of the fiscal year</li><li>Fiscal 2017 second quarter pre-tax gain on sale of the CHSA and COBRA businesses of $205 million</li></ul><p>ADP now assumes worldwide new business bookings to be about flat with the $1.75 billion sold in fiscal 2016, compared to the prior forecast of 4% to 6% growth.&#160; ADP now expects full year revenue growth of about 6% compared to our prior forecast of 7% to 8% growth.&#160; This revenue forecast continues to include about one percentage point of pressure from the disposition of our CHSA and COBRA businesses.&#160;</p><p>Reflecting the tax benefit received in the second quarter, ADP now anticipates an adjusted effective tax rate of 32.4% compared to the prior forecast of 32.7%.&#160; ADP continues to expect full year diluted earnings per share from continuing operations to grow 15% to 17%, and adjusted diluted earnings per share growth of 11% to 13%.&#160; This earnings growth forecast still assumes an adjusted EBIT margin expansion of about 50 basis points.&#160; The forecast now assumes fiscal 2017 share repurchases of $1.2 to $1.4 billion funded by existing balance sheet cash, as compared to our prior forecast of $1.0 to $1.4 billion.</p><p><u>Reportable Segments Fiscal 2017</u><u> Forecast</u></p><ul type="disc"><li>For the Employer Services segment, ADP now anticipates revenue growth of approximately 3% to 4% compared to the prior forecast of approximately 4% to 5%.&#160; ADP now expects Employer Services segment margin expansion of 25 to 50 basis points compared to our prior forecast of about 50 basis points.</li><li>ADP continues to expect pays per control to increase 2.5% for the year.</li><li>For the PEO Services segment, ADP now anticipates approximately 13% revenue growth compared to the prior forecast of 14% to 16%.&#160; ADP now expects PEO Services segment margin expansion of at least 100 basis points compared to our prior forecast of about 75 basis points.</li></ul><p><u>Client Funds Extended Investment Strategy Fiscal 2017 Forecast</u></p><p>The interest assumptions in our forecasts are based on Fed Funds futures contracts and forward yield curves as of January 30, 2017.&#160; The Fed Funds futures contracts used in the client short and corporate cash interest income forecasts assume an increase in the Fed Funds rate in June 2017.&#160; The three-and-a-half and five-year U.S. government agency rates based on the forward yield curves as of January 30, 2017 were used to forecast new purchase rates for the client and corporate extended, and client long portfolios, respectively.</p><ul type="disc"><li>Interest on funds held for clients is expected to increase $15 million, or about 4%, compared to the prior forecast of $5 to $10 million, or 2% to 3%.&#160; This is based on anticipated growth in average client funds balances of approximately 3% from $22.4 billion in fiscal 2016 and an average yield which is anticipated to be about flat at 1.7% compared to the fiscal 2016 average yield.</li><li>The total contribution from the client funds extended investment strategy is now expected to be up $10 million compared to our prior forecast of up $5 million compared with a year ago.</li></ul><p><strong>Investor Webcast Today</strong><br>ADP will host a conference call for financial analysts today, Wednesday, February 1, 2017 at 8:30 a.m. EST.&#160; The conference call will be webcast live on ADP&#8217;s website at investors.adp.com and will be available for replay following the call. A slide presentation will be available shortly before the webcast.</p><p>Supplemental financial information including schedules of quarterly and full year reportable segment revenues and earnings for fiscal years 2015 and 2016 &#160;and the first two quarters of fiscal 2017, as well as details of the first and second quarter fiscal 2017 results from the client funds extended investment strategy, are posted to ADP&#8217;s website at investors.adp.com.&#160; ADP news releases, current financial information, SEC filings and Investor Relations presentations are accessible at the same website.</p><p><strong>Non-GAAP Financial Information<br></strong>The company has presented certain financial data that are considered non-GAAP financial measures and are reconciled to their comparable GAAP measures in the accompanying financial tables.&#160; The adjusted EBIT performance measures include interest income earned on investments associated with our client funds extended investment strategy and interest expense on borrowings related to our client funds extended investment strategy.&#160; ADP believes these amounts to be fundamental to the underlying operations of our business model.&#160; ADP&#8217;s calculation of adjusted EBIT may differ from similarly titled measures used by other companies.</p><p>The presentation of growth rates on a constant dollar basis represent a non-GAAP measure and are calculated by restating current period results into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates.</p><p><strong>About ADP </strong>(Nasdaq:ADP)<br>Powerful technology plus a human touch.&#160; Companies of all types and sizes around the world rely on ADP&#8217;s cloud software and expert insights to help unlock the potential of their people. &#160;HR. Talent. Benefits. Payroll. Compliance. &#160;Working together to build a better workforce.&#160; For more information, visit ADP.com.</p><table style="border-collapse: collapse; border-collapse: collapse; border-collapse: collapse; vertical-align: bottom ; ">&#160;</td></tr><tr><td colspan="29" style="vertical-align: bottom ; ">The following table reconciles our reported results to adjusted results which exclude one or more of the following: our provision for income taxes, certain interest amounts, the charges related to our Service Alignment Initiative, the gain on the sale of our CHSA and COBRA businesses in fiscal 2017, and the gain on sale of a building and the gain on the sale of our AdvancedMD ("AMD") business in fiscal 2016. We use certain adjusted results, among other measures, to evaluate our operating performance in the absence of certain items and for planning and forecasting of future periods. We believe that the exclusion of these items helps us reflect the fundamentals of our underlying business model and analyze results against our expectations, against prior period, and to plan for future periods by focusing on our underlying operations. We believe that these adjusted results provide relevant and useful information for investors because it allows investors to view performance in a manner similar to the method used by management and improves their ability to understand and assess our operating performance. Generally, the nature of these exclusions are for specific items that are not fundamental to our underlying business operations. Specifically, we have excluded the impact of certain interest expense and certain interest income from adjusted earnings from continuing operations before interest and income taxes ("Adjusted EBIT"). We continue to include the interest income earned on investments associated with our client funds extended investment strategy and interest expense on borrowings related to our client funds extended investment strategy as we believe these amounts to be fundamental to the underlying operations of our business model. The amounts included as adjustments in the table below represent the interest income and interest expense that is not related to our client funds extended investment strategy and are labeled as "All other interest expense" and "All other interest income." The majority of charges related to our Service Alignment Initiative represent severance charges. Severance charges have been taken in the past and not included as an adjustment to get to adjusted results. Unlike severance charges in prior periods, these specific charges relate to a broad-based, company-wide Service Alignment Initiative. Since Adjusted EBIT, Adjusted provision for income taxes, Adjusted net earnings from continuing operations, Adjusted diluted earnings per share ("Adjusted diluted EPS") from continuing operations, Adjusted EBIT margin and Adjusted effective tax rate are not measures of performance calculated in accordance with U.S. GAAP, they should not be considered in isolation from, as a substitute for, or superior to earnings from continuing operations before income taxes, provision for income taxes, net earnings from continuing operations and diluted earnings per share ("Diluted EPS") from continuing operations and they may not be comparable to similarly titled measures used by other companies.<br></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: left ;
